vocs:relative vocs:w-full vocs:max-w-content vocs:space-y-6 vocs:max-md:overflow-x-hidden" data-v-content="true"><h1 data-v="" id="attach-a-transfer-memo">Attach a Transfer Memo</h1>
<p data-v="">Attach 32-byte references to <a href="/protocol/tip20/overview" data-v="true" data-v-link="true">TIP-20</a> transfers for payment reconciliation. Use memos to link onchain transactions to your internal recordsâcustomer IDs, invoice numbers, or any identifier that helps you match payments to your database.</p>

<h2 data-v="" id="steps">Steps<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/guide/payments/transfer-memos#steps" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg class="heading-anchor-icon" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.75em" height="0.75em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></a></h2>
<div data-v="true" data-v-steps="true"><div class="vocs:space-y-6" data-v-content="true"><h3 data-v="" id="set-up-your-project" data-v-step-title="true">Set up your project<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/guide/payments/transfer-memos#set-up-your-project" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg class="heading-anchor-icon" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.75em" height="0.75em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></a></h3><div data-v-step-content="true"><p data-v="">Ensure you have Wagmi configured with Tempo. Follow either guide to get started:</p><ul data-v="">
<li data-v=""><a href="/guide/use-accounts/embed-passkeys" data-v="true" data-v-link="true">Embed Passkey accounts</a></li>
<li data-v=""><a href="/guide/use-accounts/connect-to-wallets" data-v="true" data-v-link="true">Connect to wallets</a></li>
</ul></div></div><div class="vocs:space-y-6" data-v-content="true"><h3 data-v="" id="send-a-transfer-with-memo" data-v-step-title="true">Send a transfer with memo<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/guide/payments/transfer-memos#send-a-transfer-with-memo" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg class="heading-anchor-icon" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.75em" height="0.75em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></a></h3><div data-v-step-content="true"><p data-v="">Use <code data-v="true">transferWithMemo</code> to attach a reference to your payment. The memo is a 32-byte value that gets emitted in the <code data-v="true">TransferWithMemo</code> event.</p><div data-orientation="horizontal" data-activation-direction="none" data-v-code-container="true" data-v-code-group="true"><div data-orientation="horizontal" data-activation-direction="none" role="tablist" aria-label="Code group" data-v-code-header="true" <h2 data-v="" id="recipes">Recipes<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/guide/payments/transfer-memos#recipes" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg class="heading-anchor-icon" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.75em" height="0.75em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></a></h2>
<h3 data-v="" id="exchange-deposit-reconciliation">Exchange deposit reconciliation<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/guide/payments/transfer-memos#exchange-deposit-reconciliation" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg class="heading-anchor-icon" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.75em" height="0.75em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></a></h3>
<p data-v="">As an exchange, use a single master hot wallet for all customer deposits. Customers include their customer ID as the memo, and you credit their account by parsing the event.</p>
<div data-v-code-container="true"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark-dimmed vocs:relative vocs:group/code" tabindex="0" data-v="true"><code data-language="ts" data-v="true"><span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">import</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7"> { Actions } </span><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">from</span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF"> &#x27;viem/tempo&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">import</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7"> { parseUnits, stringToHex, pad } </span><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">from</span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF"> &#x27;viem&#x27;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#6A737D, #768390);--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#768390">// Customer deposits with their customer ID</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">await</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7"> Actions.token.</span><span style="color:light-dark(#6F42C1, #DCBDFB);--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#DCBDFB">transferSync</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">(walletClient, {</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">  amount: </span><span style="color:light-dark(#6F42C1, #DCBDFB);--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#DCBDFB">parseUnits</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">(</span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF">&#x27;500&#x27;</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">, </span><span style="color:light-dark(#005CC5, #6CB6FF);--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#6CB6FF">6</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">),</span></span>

<h3 data-v="" id="payroll-batch-payments">Payroll batch payments<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/guide/payments/transfer-memos#payroll-batch-payments" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg class="heading-anchor-icon" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.75em" height="0.75em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></a></h3>
<p data-v="">Batch multiple payments in a single Tempo transaction with employee IDs in each memo for clear accounting records.</p>

<h3 data-v="" id="refund-address-in-memo">Refund address in memo<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/guide/payments/transfer-memos#refund-address-in-memo" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg class="heading-anchor-icon" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.75em" height="0.75em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></a></h3>
<p data-v="">Include a refund address in the memo so the recipient knows where to send funds if a reversal is needed.</p>
<div data-v-code-container="true"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark-dimmed vocs:relative vocs:group/code" tabindex="0" data-v="true"><code data-language="ts" data-v="true"><span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">import</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7"> { Actions } </span><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">from</span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF"> &#x27;viem/tempo&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">import</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7"> { parseUnits, stringToHex, pad } </span><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">from</span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF"> &#x27;viem&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line" data-empty-line="true"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">const</span><span style="color:light-dark(#005CC5, #6CB6FF);--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#6CB6FF"> refundMemo</span><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067"> =</span><span style="color:light-dark(#6F42C1, #DCBDFB);--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#DCBDFB"> pad</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">(</span><span style="color:light-dark(#6F42C1, #DCBDFB);--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#DCBDFB">stringToHex</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">(</span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF">&#x27;REFUND 0x742d35Cc6634C0532925a3b8&#x27;</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">), { size: </span><span style="color:light-dark(#005CC5, #6CB6FF);--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#6CB6FF">32</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7"> })</span></span>
<span class="line" data-empty-line="true"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">await</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7"> Actions.token.</span><span style="color:light-dark(#6F42C1, #DCBDFB);--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#DCBDFB">transferSync</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">(walletClient, {</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">  to: merchantAddress,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">  amount: </span><span style="color:light-dark(#6F42C1, #DCBDFB);--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#DCBDFB">parseUnits</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">(</span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF">&#x27;100&#x27;</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">, </span><span style="color:light-dark(#005CC5, #6CB6FF);--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#6CB6FF">6</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">  memo: refundMemo,</span></span>

<h2 data-v="" id="best-practices">Best Practices<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/guide/payments/transfer-memos#best-practices" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg class="heading-anchor-icon" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.75em" height="0.75em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></a></h2>
<h3 data-v="" id="use-consistent-memo-formats">Use consistent memo formats<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/guide/payments/transfer-memos#use-consistent-memo-formats" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg class="heading-anchor-icon" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.75em" height="0.75em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></a></h3>
<p data-v="">Establish a naming convention for your memos (e.g., <code data-v="true">CUST-{id}</code>, <code data-v="true">INV-{number}</code>, <code data-v="true">REFUND-{id}</code>) to make parsing and filtering reliable across your system.</p>
<h3 data-v="" id="keep-memos-under-32-bytes">Keep memos under 32 bytes<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/guide/payments/transfer-memos#keep-memos-under-32-bytes" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg class="heading-anchor-icon" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.75em" height="0.75em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></a></h3>
<p data-v="">Memos are <code data-v="true">bytes32</code> values. Use <code data-v="true">toHex(string, { size: 32 })</code> to convert stringsâif your string exceeds 32 bytes, it will be truncated. For longer references, store the full data offchain and use a hash or short ID as the memo.</p>
<h3 data-v="" id="index-memos-for-efficient-queries">Index memos for efficient queries<a aria-label="Link to this section" class="heading-anchor" href="/guide/payments/transfer-memos#index-memos-for-efficient-queries" data-v-link="true" data-v="true"><svg class="heading-anchor-icon" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.75em" height="0.75em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></a></h3>
<p data-v="">The <code data-v="true">TransferWithMemo</code> event has <code data-v="true">memo</code> as an indexed parameter. Use <code data-v="true">getLogs</code> with the <code data-v="true">args</code> filter to query transactions by memo without scanning all events.</p>
<div data-v-code-container="true"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark-dimmed vocs:relative vocs:group/code" tabindex="0" data-v="true"><code data-language="ts" data-v="true"><span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">import</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7"> { parseAbiItem, stringToHex, pad } </span><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">from</span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF"> &#x27;viem&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line" data-empty-line="true"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067">const</span><span style="color:light-dark(#005CC5, #6CB6FF);--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#6CB6FF"> logs</span><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067"> =</span><span style="color:light-dark(#D73A49, #F47067);--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F47067"> await</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7"> client.</span><span style="color:light-dark(#6F42C1, #DCBDFB);--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#DCBDFB">getLogs</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">  address: tokenAddress,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">  event: </span><span style="color:light-dark(#6F42C1, #DCBDFB);--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#DCBDFB">parseAbiItem</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">(</span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF">&#x27;event TransferWithMemo(address indexed from, address indexed to, uint256 value, bytes32 indexed memo)&#x27;</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">  args: { memo: </span><span style="color:light-dark(#6F42C1, #DCBDFB);--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#DCBDFB">pad</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">(</span><span style="color:light-dark(#6F42C1, #DCBDFB);--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#DCBDFB">stringToHex</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">(</span><span style="color:light-dark(#032F62, #96D0FF);--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#96D0FF">&#x27;INV-12345&#x27;</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7">), { size: </span><span style="color:light-dark(#005CC5, #6CB6FF);--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#6CB6FF">32</span><span style="color:light-dark(#24292E, #ADBAC7);--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#ADBAC7"> }) },</span></span>
